---
layout: paradigm
paradigm: PROPN_SEIKKAILU
---
### ` PROPN_SEIKKAILU `

* _Proper noun u stem, no variations_
* Universal POS is PROPN and legacy POS is NOUN
* suffixes use back vowel harmony
* KOTUS paradigm used in their dictionary is 2
* The lemmas must end in * None * (which will be deleted to form an invariant stub) and the regex matching the lemma is ` u `
